<rate>5<//rate><text>Last year I was struggling on finding the perfect tux for my wedding. The Men's Wearhouse tuxes were too chintzy and the suits at places like Neiman Marcus were way too expensive for the quality. I also wanted a suit that was custom-made to fit me perfectly.

I googled around and landed on Hall Madden. I set up an appointment online to go check it out. Andrew greeted me at the door and knew exactly the type of tux I was looking for. He really seemed to care that I would look my best and made sure to get the details of the wedding so we could optimize the suit's look and comfort for that moment.

We flipped through a book of fabrics and Andrew explained the pros and cons of each, with regards to cost, quality, and how they would look in pictures. I settled on the Loro Piana fabric, as it was the darkest and looked and felt the best to me. At a later appointment the crew took my measurements and even made special note of my slightly uneven shoulder heights.

What is great about the Hall Madden process is that they first will build a test suit so that they can make sure their measurements were 100% accurate. At the test suit fitting they realized that there were some slight adjustments that needed to be made to the pants and waist of the suit. The custom dresshirt fit perfectly first try! They explained that the test suit was made from less expensive fabric and that it would be donated to those in need - I thought that was great.

When I came back for the final fitting I was amazed. I put on the suit and instantly knew it was right. The fabric and tailoring made the suit extremely comfortable to wear - it felt like wearing Lululemon pants. The color of the fabric was perfect! I even got my last name embroidered underneath the collar, which I thought was a cool customization.

At the wedding I received tons of compliments and looked great in the pictures. I was also able to comfortably bust some moves on the dance floor. I think I may have danced a little too hard because I noticed sometime later that part of the seam of the arm inlay had gotten unsewn. I sent an email to Andrew about a year after the wedding and he said to stop by so he could check it out. When I visited he immediately dropped what he was doing and examined the damage. We took a short walk down to a tailor that Hall Madden partners with and Andrew was able to get my suit repaired for free within a few minutes! Before I left he also handed me some collar stays because I had misplaced mine. He really went above and beyond what I expected as a customer and it made me feel great.

These are guys who are there for you and are genuinely interested in giving you the best suit of your life. I can't thank them enough! If you want to work with someone who will be your friend through the entire bespoke suit process, then do yourself a favor and go to Hall Madden!<//text>< Pictures>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
Sonic has more variety than most fast food places, and they've tried to capture, to some extent, the nostalgic feeling some of us old-timers remember from the drive-ins we used to go to. The high-tech ordering stations flanking each parking space can be intimidating the first time you try to use them, however.  For those who have less time on their hands, they also offer drive-thru service. Their prices are pretty reasonable, as fast food goes.  But a "famous root beer stand" they are not.</review>
